The_DT results_NNS of_IN the_DT work_NN shown_VBN as_IN performed_VBN at_IN dispensaries_NNS are_VBP better_RB in_IN every_DT way_NN than_IN those_DT of_IN the_DT previous_JJ year_NN ._.

5_CD ._.
The_DT inspection_NN work_NN done_VBN by_IN District_NNP Superintendents_NNP was_VBD fairty_JJ satis-_JJ factory_NN ._.

The_DT Resident_NNP has_VBZ ,_, in_IN reviewing_VBG the_DT two_CD preceding_NN reports_NNS ,_, specially_RB called_VBD the_DT attention_NN of_IN Civil_NNP Surgeons_NNP to_TO this_DT im-_JJ portant_NN duty_NN ._.

of_IN the_DT vaccine_NN operations_NNS performed_VBD at_IN dispensaries_NNS ,_, and_CC the_DT Resident_NNP expects_VBZ this_DT duty_NN to_TO be_VB fully_RB carried_VBN out_RP in_IN future_JJ ._.
